"""
URL configuration for logistica project.

The `urlpatterns` list routes URLs to views. For more information please see:
    https://docs.djangoproject.com/en/4.2/topics/http/urls/
Examples:
Function views
    1. Add an import:  from my_app import views
    2. Add a URL to urlpatterns:  path('', views.home, name='home')
Class-based views
    1. Add an import:  from other_app.views import Home
    2. Add a URL to urlpatterns:  path('', Home.as_view(), name='home')
Including another URLconf
    1. Import the include() function: from django.urls import include, path
    2. Add a URL to urlpatterns:  path('blog/', include('blog.urls'))
"""
from django.contrib import admin
from django.urls import path, include
from django.conf import settings
from django.conf.urls.static import static

urlpatterns = [
    path('admin/', admin.site.urls),
    path('', include('transporte.urls')),  # Esto incluye todas las URLs de transporte
]

# Solo en desarrollo para servir archivos est√°ticos
if settings.DEBUG:
    urlpatterns += static(settings.STATIC_URL, document_root=settings.STATIC_ROOT)

===== admin.py =====
from django.contrib import admin
from .models import *

@admin.register(Ruta)
class RutaAdmin(admin.ModelAdmin):
    list_display = ['origen', 'destino', 'tipo_transporte', 'distancia_km']

@admin.register(Vehiculo)
class VehiculoAdmin(admin.ModelAdmin):
    list_display = ['patente', 'tipo_vehiculo', 'modelo', 'capacidad_kg', 'activo']

@admin.register(Aeronave)
class AeronaveAdmin(admin.ModelAdmin):
    list_display = ['matricula', 'tipo_aeronave', 'modelo', 'capacidad_kg', 'activo']

@admin.register(Conductor)
class ConductorAdmin(admin.ModelAdmin):
    list_display = ['nombre', 'rut', 'licencia', 'activo']

@admin.register(Piloto)
class PilotoAdmin(admin.ModelAdmin):
    list_display = ['nombre', 'rut', 'certificacion', 'horas_vuelo', 'activo']

@admin.register(Cliente)
class ClienteAdmin(admin.ModelAdmin):
    list_display = ['razon_social', 'rut', 'persona_contacto', 'activo']

@admin.register(Carga)
class CargaAdmin(admin.ModelAdmin):
    list_display = ['descripcion', 'tipo_carga', 'peso_kg', 'cliente']

@admin.register(Seguro)
class SeguroAdmin(admin.ModelAdmin):
    list_display = ['numero_poliza', 'tipo_seguro', 'aseguradora', 'estado']

@admin.register(Despacho)
class DespachoAdmin(admin.ModelAdmin):
    list_display = ['id', 'ruta', 'estado', 'costo_envio', 'fecha_despacho']

===== models.py =====
from django.db import models
from django.core.validators import MinValueValidator

class TipoTransporte(models.TextChoices):
    TERRESTRE = 'TERRESTRE', 'Terrestre'
    AEREO = 'AEREO', 'A√©reo'

class EstadoDespacho(models.TextChoices):
    PENDIENTE = 'PENDIENTE', 'Pendiente'
    EN_RUTA = 'EN_RUTA', 'En Ruta'
    ENTREGADO = 'ENTREGADO', 'Entregado'
    CANCELADO = 'CANCELADO', 'Cancelado'

class Ruta(models.Model):
    origen = models.CharField(max_length=100)
    destino = models.CharField(max_length=100)
    tipo_transporte = models.CharField(max_length=10, choices=TipoTransporte.choices)
    distancia_km = models.FloatField(validators=[MinValueValidator(0)])
    
    def __str__(self):
        return f"{self.origen} - {self.destino}"

class Vehiculo(models.Model):
    patente = models.CharField(max_length=10, unique=True)
    tipo_vehiculo = models.CharField(max_length=50)
    modelo = models.CharField(max_length=50)
    capacidad_kg = models.IntegerField(validators=[MinValueValidator(0)])
    a√±o = models.IntegerField()
    conductor_asignado = models.ForeignKey('Conductor', on_delete=models.SET_NULL, null=True, blank=True)
    activo = models.BooleanField(default=True)
    
    def __str__(self):
        return f"{self.patente} - {self.modelo}"

class Aeronave(models.Model):
    matricula = models.CharField(max_length=10, unique=True)
    tipo_aeronave = models.CharField(max_length=50)
    modelo = models.CharField(max_length=50)
    capacidad_kg = models.IntegerField(validators=[MinValueValidator(0)])
    piloto_asignado = models.ForeignKey('Piloto', on_delete=models.SET_NULL, null=True, blank=True)
    activo = models.BooleanField(default=True)
    
    def __str__(self):
        return f"{self.matricula} - {self.modelo}"

class Conductor(models.Model):
    nombre = models.CharField(max_length=100)
    rut = models.CharField(max_length=12, unique=True)
    licencia = models.CharField(max_length=10)
    telefono = models.CharField(max_length=15)
    email = models.EmailField()
    activo = models.BooleanField(default=True)
    
    def __str__(self):
        return f"{self.nombre} ({self.licencia})"

class Piloto(models.Model):
    nombre = models.CharField(max_length=100)
    rut = models.CharField(max_length=12, unique=True)
    certificacion = models.CharField(max_length=20)
    telefono = models.CharField(max_length=15)
    email = models.EmailField()
    horas_vuelo = models.IntegerField(default=0)
    activo = models.BooleanField(default=True)
    
    def __str__(self):
        return f"{self.nombre} ({self.certificacion})"

class Cliente(models.Model):
    razon_social = models.CharField(max_length=200)
    rut = models.CharField(max_length=12, unique=True)
    persona_contacto = models.CharField(max_length=100)
    telefono = models.CharField(max_length=15)
    email = models.EmailField()
    direccion = models.TextField()
    activo = models.BooleanField(default=True)
    
    def __str__(self):
        return self.razon_social

class Carga(models.Model):
    descripcion = models.CharField(max_length=200)
    tipo_carga = models.CharField(max_length=50)
    peso_kg = models.FloatField(validators=[MinValueValidator(0)])
    volumen_m3 = models.FloatField(validators=[MinValueValidator(0)])
    valor_declarado = models.DecimalField(max_digits=12, decimal_places=2)
    cliente = models.ForeignKey(Cliente, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    notas_especiales = models.TextField(blank=True)
    
    def __str__(self):
        return f"{self.descripcion} - {self.cliente}"

class Seguro(models.Model):
    numero_poliza = models.CharField(max_length=50, unique=True)
    tipo_seguro = models.CharField(max_length=50)
    vehiculo = models.ForeignKey(Vehiculo, on_delete=models.CASCADE, null=True, blank=True)
    aeronave = models.ForeignKey(Aeronave, on_delete=models.CASCADE, null=True, blank=True)
    aseguradora = models.CharField(max_length=100)
    cobertura = models.DecimalField(max_digits=12, decimal_places=2)
    vigencia_desde = models.DateField()
    vigencia_hasta = models.DateField()
    estado = models.CharField(max_length=20)
    
    def __str__(self):
        return f"{self.numero_poliza} - {self.aseguradora}"

class Despacho(models.Model):
    fecha_despacho = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
    estado = models.CharField(max_length=10, choices=EstadoDespacho.choices, default=EstadoDespacho.PENDIENTE)
    costo_envio = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    ruta = models.ForeignKey(Ruta, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    vehiculo = models.ForeignKey(Vehiculo, on_delete=models.SET_NULL, null=True, blank=True)
    aeronave = models.ForeignKey(Aeronave, on_delete=models.SET_NULL, null=True, blank=True)
    conductor = models.ForeignKey(Conductor, on_delete=models.SET_NULL, null=True, blank=True)
    piloto = models.ForeignKey(Piloto, on_delete=models.SET_NULL, null=True, blank=True)
    carga = models.ForeignKey(Carga, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    cliente = models.ForeignKey(Cliente, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    
    def __str__(self):
        return f"Despacho {self.id} - {self.ruta}"
============================================================


===== serializers.py =====
from rest_framework import serializers
from .models import *

class RutaSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Ruta
        fields = '__all__'

class VehiculoSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Vehiculo
        fields = '__all__'

class AeronaveSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Aeronave
        fields = '__all__'

class ConductorSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Conductor
        fields = '__all__'

class PilotoSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Piloto
        fields = '__all__'

class ClienteSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Cliente
        fields = '__all__'

class CargaSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Carga
        fields = '__all__'

class SeguroSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Seguro
        fields = '__all__'

class DespachoSerializer(serializers.ModelSerializer):
    class Meta:
        model = Despacho
        fields = '__all__'

===== urls.py =====
from django.urls import path, include
from rest_framework.routers import DefaultRouter
from . import views

# Crear el router para las API views
router = DefaultRouter()
router.register(r'rutas', views.RutaViewSet)
router.register(r'vehiculos', views.VehiculoViewSet)
router.register(r'aeronaves', views.AeronaveViewSet)
router.register(r'conductores', views.ConductorViewSet)
router.register(r'pilotos', views.PilotoViewSet)
router.register(r'clientes', views.ClienteViewSet)
router.register(r'cargas', views.CargaViewSet)
router.register(r'seguros', views.SeguroViewSet)
router.register(r'despachos', views.DespachoViewSet)

# URLs para las vistas de templates
urlpatterns = [
    # API URLs
    path('api/', include(router.urls)),
    
    # Template URLs
    path('', views.dashboard, name='dashboard'),
    path('despachos/', views.despachos_view, name='despachos'),
    path('vehiculos/', views.vehiculos_view, name='vehiculos'),
    path('aeronaves/', views.aeronaves_view, name='aeronaves'),
    path('conductores/', views.conductores_view, name='conductores'),
    path('pilotos/', views.pilotos_view, name='pilotos'),
    path('clientes/', views.clientes_view, name='clientes'),
    path('cargas/', views.cargas_view, name='cargas'),
    path('seguros/', views.seguros_view, name='seguros'),
    path('reportes/', views.reportes_view, name='reportes'),
    path('api-docs/', views.api_view, name='api'),
]

===== views.py =====
from rest_framework import viewsets
from .models import *
from .serializers import *

class RutaViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Ruta.objects.all()
    serializer_class = RutaSerializer

class VehiculoViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Vehiculo.objects.all()
    serializer_class = VehiculoSerializer

class AeronaveViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Aeronave.objects.all()
    serializer_class = AeronaveSerializer

class ConductorViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Conductor.objects.all()
    serializer_class = ConductorSerializer

class PilotoViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Piloto.objects.all()
    serializer_class = PilotoSerializer

class ClienteViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Cliente.objects.all()
    serializer_class = ClienteSerializer

class CargaViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Carga.objects.all()
    serializer_class = CargaSerializer

class SeguroViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Seguro.objects.all()
    serializer_class = SeguroSerializer

class DespachoViewSet(viewsets.ModelViewSet):
    queryset = Despacho.objects.all()
    serializer_class = DespachoSerializer

# Vistas para templates HTML
from django.shortcuts import render

def dashboard(request):
    return render(request, 'transporte/dashboard.html')

def despachos_view(request):
    return render(request, 'transporte/despachos.html')

def vehiculos_view(request):
    return render(request, 'transporte/vehiculos.html')

def aeronaves_view(request):
    return render(request, 'transporte/aeronaves.html')

def conductores_view(request):
    return render(request, 'transporte/conductores.html')

def pilotos_view(request):
    return render(request, 'transporte/pilotos.html')

def clientes_view(request):
    return render(request, 'transporte/clientes.html')

def cargas_view(request):
    return render(request, 'transporte/cargas.html')

    return render(request, 'transporte/seguros.html')

    return render(request, 'transporte/api.html')

    <script>
        function showModal(modalId) {
            document.getElementById(modalId).style.display = 'block';
        }

        function closeModal(modalId) {
            document.getElementById(modalId).style.display = 'none';
        }

        function showNewConductorModal() {
            showModal('newConductorModal');
        }

        function viewConductor(conductorId) {
            const content = `
                <div style="line-height: 1.6;">
                    <p><strong>ID:</strong> ${conductorId}</p>
                    <p><strong>Nombre:</strong> Carlos L√≥pez</p>
                    <p><strong>Licencia:</strong> A1-A3</p>
                    <p><strong>Vence Licencia:</strong> 15/06/2024</p>
                    <p><strong>Tel√©fono:</strong> +56 9 1234 5678</p>
                    <p><strong>Email:</strong> carlos.lopez@empresa.com</p>
                    <p><strong>Veh√≠culo Asignado:</strong> ABC-123 (Volvo FH16)</p>
                    <p><strong>Estado:</strong> <span class="badge active">Activo</span></p>
                    <div style="margin-top: 1.5rem;">
                        <h4>Estad√≠sticas</h4>
                        <ul style="margin-top: 0.5rem;">
                            <li>Despachos este mes: 12</li>
                            <li>Kil√≥metros recorridos: 4,250 km</li>
                            <li>Calificaci√≥n promedio: 4.8/5</li>
                            <li>Incidentes: 0</li>
                        </ul>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
            document.getElementById('viewConductorTitle').textContent = `Conductor ${conductorId}`;
            document.getElementById('viewConductorContent').innerHTML = content;
            showModal('viewConductorModal');
        }

        function editConductor(conductorId) {
            showNotification(`Editando conductor ${conductorId}...`);
        }

        document.getElementById('newConductorForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            showNotification('Conductor creado exitosamente');
            closeModal('newConductorModal');
        });

        function showNotification(message) {
            const notification = document.createElement('div');
            notification.textContent = `‚úì ${message}`;
            notification.style.cssText = `
                position: fixed;
                top: 20px;
                right: 20px;
                background: linear-gradient(135deg, #6366f1, #06b6d4);
                color: white;
                padding: 1rem 2rem;
                border-radius: 12px;
                box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(99, 102, 241, 0.4);
                z-index: 1000;
                animation: slideInRight 0.4s ease-out;
                font-weight: 600;
            `;
            
            document.body.appendChild(notification);
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                notification.style.animation = 'slideOutRight 0.4s ease-out';
                setTimeout(() => notification.remove(), 400);
            }, 3000);
        }

        const style = document.createElement('style');
        style.textContent = `
            @keyframes slideInRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
            }
            @keyframes slideOutRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
            }
        `;
        document.head.appendChild(style);

        window.onclick = function(event) {
            const modals = document.querySelectorAll('.modal');
            modals.forEach(modal => {
                if (event.target === modal) {
                    modal.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
        }

        console.log('üë®‚Äçüíº M√≥dulo de Conductores cargado exitosamente');
    </script>

        function testAPI() {
            showNotification('Probando conexi√≥n API...');
            // Simulate API test
            setTimeout(() => {
                showNotification('‚úì Conexi√≥n API exitosa - JWT activo');
            }, 1500);
        }

        function showDocumentation() {
            showNotification('Abriendo documentaci√≥n completa de la API...');
            // In a real application, this would open the full API documentation
        }

        function generateAPIKey() {
            showNotification('Generando nueva clave API...');
            // In a real application, this would generate a new API key
            setTimeout(() => {
                showNotification('‚úì Nueva clave API generada exitosamente');
            }, 2000);
        }

        function viewAPIKey(keyId) {
            showNotification(`Mostrando detalles de clave API: ${keyId}`);
            // In a real application, this would show the API key details
        }

        function revokeAPIKey(keyId) {
            if (confirm(`¬øEst√° seguro de que desea revocar la clave API ${keyId}?`)) {
                showNotification(`Revocando clave API: ${keyId}`);
                // In a real application, this would revoke the API key
                setTimeout(() => {
                    showNotification('‚úì Clave API revocada exitosamente');
                }, 2000);
            }
        }

        function showNotification(message) {
            const notification = document.createElement('div');
            notification.textContent = `‚úì ${message}`;
            notification.style.cssText = `
                position: fixed;
                top: 20px;
                right: 20px;
                background: linear-gradient(135deg, #6366f1, #06b6d4);
                color: white;
                padding: 1rem 2rem;
                border-radius: 12px;
                box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(99, 102, 241, 0.4);
                z-index: 1000;
                animation: slideInRight 0.4s ease-out;
                font-weight: 600;
            `;
            
            document.body.appendChild(notification);
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                notification.style.animation = 'slideOutRight 0.4s ease-out';
                setTimeout(() => notification.remove(), 400);
            }, 3000);
        }

        const style = document.createElement('style');
        style.textContent = `
            @keyframes slideInRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
            }
            @keyframes slideOutRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
            }
        `;
        document.head.appendChild(style);

        console.log('üîó M√≥dulo de API cargado exitosamente');
        console.log('üìä Sistema integrado con Django REST Framework');
        console.log('üîê Autenticaci√≥n JWT activa');
        console.log('üöÄ API REST operativa');
    </script>

    <script>
        function showModal(modalId) {
            document.getElementById(modalId).style.display = 'block';
        }

        function closeModal(modalId) {
            document.getElementById(modalId).style.display = 'none';
        }

        function showNewCargaModal() {
            showModal('newCargaModal');
        }

        function viewCarga(cargaId) {
            const content = `
                <div style="line-height: 1.6;">
                    <p><strong>ID:</strong> ${cargaId}</p>
                    <p><strong>Descripci√≥n:</strong> Electr√≥nicos de consumo</p>
                    <p><strong>Tipo:</strong> General</p>
                    <p><strong>Peso:</strong> 850 kg</p>
                    <p><strong>Volumen:</strong> 12 m¬≥</p>
                    <p><strong>Valor Declarado:</strong> $25,000</p>
                    <p><strong>Cliente:</strong> TechCorp S.A.</p>
                    <p><strong>Estado:</strong> <span class="badge active">Entregado</span></p>
                    <p><strong>Notas Especiales:</strong> Manejar con cuidado, productos fr√°giles</p>
                    <div style="margin-top: 1.5rem;">
                        <h4>Informaci√≥n de Transporte</h4>
                        <ul style="margin-top: 0.5rem;">
                            <li>Despacho Asignado: D-2042</li>
                            <li>Veh√≠culo: ABC-123</li>
                            <li>Conductor: Carlos L√≥pez</li>
                            <li>Fecha de Entrega: 10/12/2023</li>
                        </ul>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
            document.getElementById('viewCargaTitle').textContent = `Carga ${cargaId}`;
            document.getElementById('viewCargaContent').innerHTML = content;
            showModal('viewCargaModal');
        }

        function editCarga(cargaId) {
            showNotification(`Editando carga ${cargaId}...`);
        }

        document.getElementById('newCargaForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            showNotification('Carga creada exitosamente');
            closeModal('newCargaModal');
        });

        function showNotification(message) {
            const notification = document.createElement('div');
            notification.textContent = `‚úì ${message}`;
            notification.style.cssText = `
                position: fixed;
                top: 20px;
                right: 20px;
                background: linear-gradient(135deg, #6366f1, #06b6d4);
                color: white;
                padding: 1rem 2rem;
                border-radius: 12px;
                box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(99, 102, 241, 0.4);
                z-index: 1000;
                animation: slideInRight 0.4s ease-out;
                font-weight: 600;
            `;
            
            document.body.appendChild(notification);
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                notification.style.animation = 'slideOutRight 0.4s ease-out';
                setTimeout(() => notification.remove(), 400);
            }, 3000);
        }

        const style = document.createElement('style');
        style.textContent = `
            @keyframes slideInRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
            }
            @keyframes slideOutRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
            }
        `;
        document.head.appendChild(style);

        window.onclick = function(event) {
            const modals = document.querySelectorAll('.modal');
            modals.forEach(modal => {
                if (event.target === modal) {
                    modal.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
        }

        console.log('üì¶ M√≥dulo de Cargas cargado exitosamente');
    </script>
</body>

    <script>
        function showModal(modalId) {
            document.getElementById(modalId).style.display = 'block';
        }

        function closeModal(modalId) {
            document.getElementById(modalId).style.display = 'none';
        }

        function showNewClienteModal() {
            showModal('newClienteModal');
        }

        function toggleClienteFields(tipo) {
            const empresaFields = document.getElementById('empresaFields');
            const individualFields = document.getElementById('individualFields');
            
            if (tipo === 'empresa') {
                empresaFields.style.display = 'block';
                individualFields.style.display = 'none';
            } else if (tipo === 'individual') {
                empresaFields.style.display = 'none';
                individualFields.style.display = 'block';
            } else {
                empresaFields.style.display = 'none';
                individualFields.style.display = 'none';
            }
        }

        function viewCliente(clienteId) {
            const content = `
                <div style="line-height: 1.6;">
                    <p><strong>ID:</strong> ${clienteId}</p>
                    <p><strong>Raz√≥n Social:</strong> TechCorp S.A.</p>
                    <p><strong>RUT:</strong> 76.543.210-1</p>
                    <p><strong>Persona de Contacto:</strong> Juan P√©rez</p>
                    <p><strong>Tel√©fono:</strong> +56 2 2345 6789</p>
                    <p><strong>Email:</strong> juan.perez@techcorp.cl</p>
                    <p><strong>Direcci√≥n:</strong> Av. Principal 123, Santiago</p>
                    <p><strong>Estado:</strong> <span class="badge active">Activo</span></p>
                    <div style="margin-top: 1.5rem;">
                        <h4>Estad√≠sticas</h4>
                        <ul style="margin-top: 0.5rem;">
                            <li>Despachos este mes: 15</li>
                            <li>Total despachos: 245</li>
                            <li>Facturaci√≥n mensual: $1.2M</li>
                            <li>Calificaci√≥n: 4.7/5</li>
                        </ul>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
            document.getElementById('viewClienteTitle').textContent = `Cliente ${clienteId}`;
            document.getElementById('viewClienteContent').innerHTML = content;
            showModal('viewClienteModal');
        }

        function editCliente(clienteId) {
            showNotification(`Editando cliente ${clienteId}...`);
        }

        document.getElementById('newClienteForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            showNotification('Cliente creado exitosamente');
            closeModal('newClienteModal');
        });

        function showNotification(message) {
            const notification = document.createElement('div');
            notification.textContent = `‚úì ${message}`;
            notification.style.cssText = `
                position: fixed;
                top: 20px;
                right: 20px;
                background: linear-gradient(135deg, #6366f1, #06b6d4);
                color: white;
                padding: 1rem 2rem;
                border-radius: 12px;
                box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(99, 102, 241, 0.4);
                z-index: 1000;
                animation: slideInRight 0.4s ease-out;
                font-weight: 600;
            `;
            
            document.body.appendChild(notification);
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                notification.style.animation = 'slideOutRight 0.4s ease-out';
                setTimeout(() => notification.remove(), 400);
            }, 3000);
        }

        const style = document.createElement('style');
        style.textContent = `
            @keyframes slideInRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
            }
            @keyframes slideOutRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
            }
        `;
        document.head.appendChild(style);

        window.onclick = function(event) {
            const modals = document.querySelectorAll('.modal');
            modals.forEach(modal => {
                if (event.target === modal) {
                    modal.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
        }

        console.log('üë• M√≥dulo de Clientes cargado exitosamente');
    </script>

    <script>
        // Navigation Functions
        function goToDashboard() {
            window.location.href = 'dashboard.html';
        }

        function goToPage(page) {
            // Redirecci√≥n real a la p√°gina
            window.location.href = page;
        }

        // Modal Functions
        function showModal(modalId) {
            document.getElementById(modalId).style.display = 'block';
        }

        function closeModal(modalId) {
            document.getElementById(modalId).style.display = 'none';
        }

        function showNewConductorModal() {
            showModal('newConductorModal');
        }

        // View Conductor Details
        function viewConductor(conductorId) {
            const content = `
                <div style="line-height: 1.6;">
                    <p><strong>ID:</strong> ${conductorId}</p>
                    <p><strong>Nombre:</strong> Carlos L√≥pez</p>
                    <p><strong>Licencia:</strong> A1-A3</p>
                    <p><strong>Vence Licencia:</strong> 15/06/2024</p>
                    <p><strong>Tel√©fono:</strong> +56 9 1234 5678</p>
                    <p><strong>Email:</strong> carlos.lopez@empresa.com</p>
                    <p><strong>Direcci√≥n:</strong> Av. Principal 123, Santiago</p>
                    <p><strong>Veh√≠culo Asignado:</strong> ABC-123 (Volvo FH16)</p>
                    <p><strong>Estado:</strong> <span class="badge active">Activo</span></p>
                    <div style="margin-top: 1.5rem;">
                        <h4>Estad√≠sticas</h4>
                        <ul style="margin-top: 0.5rem;">
                            <li>Despachos este mes: 12</li>
                            <li>Kil√≥metros recorridos: 4,250 km</li>
                            <li>Calificaci√≥n promedio: 4.8/5</li>
                            <li>Incidentes: 0</li>
                            <li>Horas de conducci√≥n: 145 hrs</li>
                        </ul>
                    </div>

                        <h4>Certificaciones</h4>
                        <ul style="margin-top: 0.5rem;">

                        </ul>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
            document.getElementById('viewConductorTitle').textContent = `Conductor ${conductorId}`;
            document.getElementById('viewConductorContent').innerHTML = content;
            showModal('viewConductorModal');
        }

        // Edit Conductor
        function editConductor(conductorId) {
            showNotification(`Editando conductor ${conductorId}...`);
            // In a real application, this would load the edit form with existing data
        }

        // Form Submission
        document.getElementById('newConductorForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            showNotification('Conductor creado exitosamente');
            closeModal('newConductorModal');
            // In a real application, this would submit the form data to the server
        });

        // Notification System
        function showNotification(message) {
            const notification = document.createElement('div');
            notification.textContent = `‚úì ${message}`;
            notification.style.cssText = `
                position: fixed;
                top: 20px;
                right: 20px;
                background: linear-gradient(135deg, #6366f1, #06b6d4);
                color: white;
                padding: 1rem 2rem;
                border-radius: 12px;
                box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(99, 102, 241, 0.4);
                z-index: 1000;
                animation: slideInRight 0.4s ease-out;
                font-weight: 600;
            `;
            
            document.body.appendChild(notification);
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                notification.style.animation = 'slideOutRight 0.4s ease-out';
                setTimeout(() => notification.remove(), 400);
            }, 3000);
        }

        // Add slide animations
        const style = document.createElement('style');
        style.textContent = `
            @keyframes slideInRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
            }
            @keyframes slideOutRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
            }
        `;
        document.head.appendChild(style);

        // Close modal when clicking outside
        window.onclick = function(event) {
            const modals = document.querySelectorAll('.modal');
            modals.forEach(modal => {
                if (event.target === modal) {
                    modal.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
        }

        // Simulate real-time updates
        function simulateRealTimeUpdate() {
            const badges = document.querySelectorAll('.badge');
            setInterval(() => {
                const randomBadge = badges[Math.floor(Math.random() * badges.length)];
                const currentStatus = randomBadge.textContent;
                const statuses = ['Activo', 'Vacaciones', 'Licencia', 'Inactivo'];
                const newStatus = statuses[Math.floor(Math.random() * statuses.length)];
                
                if (currentStatus !== newStatus) {
                    randomBadge.textContent = newStatus;
                    
                    // Update badge class based on status
                    randomBadge.className = 'badge';
                    if (newStatus === 'Activo') randomBadge.classList.add('active');
                    else if (newStatus === 'Vacaciones') randomBadge.classList.add('warning');
                    else if (newStatus === 'Licencia') randomBadge.classList.add('alert');
                    else if (newStatus === 'Inactivo') randomBadge.classList.add('pending');
                    
                    randomBadge.style.transform = 'scale(1.2)';
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        randomBadge.style.transform = 'scale(1)';
                    }, 300);
                }
            }, 15000);
        }

        simulateRealTimeUpdate();

        console.log('üë®‚Äçüíº M√≥dulo de Conductores cargado exitosamente');
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <script>
        // Navigation Functions
        function goToDashboard() {
            // Since we're already on the dashboard, just show a notification
            showNotification('Ya est√°s en el Dashboard');
        }

        function goToPage(page) {
            // Redirecci√≥n real a la p√°gina
            window.location.href = page;
        }

        // Notification System
        function showNotification(message) {
            const notification = document.createElement('div');
            notification.textContent = `‚úì ${message}`;
            notification.style.cssText = `
                position: fixed;
                top: 20px;
                right: 20px;
                background: linear-gradient(135deg, #6366f1, #06b6d4);
                color: white;
                padding: 1rem 2rem;
                border-radius: 12px;
                box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(99, 102, 241, 0.4);
                z-index: 1000;
                animation: slideInRight 0.4s ease-out;
                font-weight: 600;
            `;
            
            document.body.appendChild(notification);
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                notification.style.animation = 'slideOutRight 0.4s ease-out';
                setTimeout(() => notification.remove(), 400);
            }, 3000);
        }

        // Add slide animations
        const style = document.createElement('style');
        style.textContent = `
            @keyframes slideInRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
            }
            @keyframes slideOutRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
            }
        `;
        document.head.appendChild(style);

        // Interactive chart bars
        document.querySelectorAll('.chart-bar').forEach((bar, index) => {
            bar.addEventListener('click', () => {
                const months = ['Ene', 'Feb', 'Mar', 'Abr', 'May', 'Jun'];
                showNotification(`${months[index]}: ${Math.floor(Math.random() * 100 + 50)} despachos`);
            });
        });

        // Modal Functions
        function showModal(title, content) {
            document.getElementById('modalTitle').textContent = title;
            document.getElementById('modalContent').innerHTML = content;
            document.getElementById('detailsModal').style.display = 'block';
        }

        function closeModal() {
            document.getElementById('detailsModal').style.display = 'none';
        }

        // Specific Detail Functions
        function showInsuranceDetails(vehicleId) {
            const content = `
                <div style="line-height: 1.6;">
                    <p><strong>Veh√≠culo:</strong> ${vehicleId}</p>
                    <p><strong>Tipo:</strong> Cami√≥n de Carga</p>
                    <p><strong>Aseguradora:</strong> Seguros Chile</p>
                    <p><strong>P√≥liza:</strong> #SC-2023-${vehicleId}</p>
                    <p><strong>Vencimiento:</strong> 15/12/2023</p>
                    <p><strong>Estado:</strong> <span style="color: var(--danger);">Vencido</span></p>
                    <p><strong>Cobertura:</strong> $500,000</p>
                    <div style="margin-top: 1rem;">
                        <button onclick="renewInsurance('${vehicleId}')" style="background: var(--primary); color: white; border: none; padding: 0.5rem 1rem; border-radius: 8px; cursor: pointer;">Renovar Seguro</button>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
            showModal(`Detalles de Seguro - ${vehicleId}`, content);
        }

        function showDespachoDetails(despachoId) {
            const content = `
                <div style="line-height: 1.6;">
                    <p><strong>Despacho:</strong> ${despachoId}</p>
                    <p><strong>Ruta:</strong> Santiago - Valpara√≠so</p>
                    <p><strong>Veh√≠culo:</strong> CAM-789</p>
                    <p><strong>Conductor:</strong> Carlos L√≥pez</p>
                    <p><strong>Carga:</strong> Electr√≥nicos - 850kg</p>
                    <p><strong>Estado:</strong> <span style="color: var(--success);">Completado</span></p>
                    <p><strong>Fecha Entrega:</strong> 10/12/2023 14:30</p>
                    <p><strong>Costo:</strong> $250,000</p>
                </div>
            `;
            showModal(`Detalles de Despacho - ${despachoId}`, content);
        }

        function showMaintenanceDetails(aeronaveId) {
            const content = `
                <div style="line-height: 1.6;">
                    <p><strong>Aeronave:</strong> ${aeronaveId}</p>
                    <p><strong>Tipo:</strong> Avi√≥n Carga</p>
                    <p><strong>Mantenimiento:</strong> Revisi√≥n Anual</p>
                    <p><strong>Programado:</strong> 20/12/2023</p>
                    <p><strong>Proveedor:</strong> Mantenimiento A√©reo S.A.</p>
                    <p><strong>Estado:</strong> <span style="color: var(--warning);">Programado</span></p>
                    <p><strong>Duraci√≥n Estimada:</strong> 3 d√≠as</p>
                    <div style="margin-top: 1rem;">
                        <button onclick="rescheduleMaintenance('${aeronaveId}')" style="background: var(--warning); color: white; border: none; padding: 0.5rem 1rem; border-radius: 8px; cursor: pointer;">Reprogramar</button>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
            showModal(`Mantenimiento - ${aeronaveId}`, content);
        }

        // Action Functions
        function createNewDespacho() {
            showNotification('Creando nuevo despacho...');
            // Simulate API call to create new dispatch
            setTimeout(() => {
                showModal('Nuevo Despacho', `
                    <div style="line-height: 1.6;">
                        <p>Formulario para crear nuevo despacho:</p>
                        <ul>
                            <li>Seleccionar Ruta</li>
                            <li>Asignar Veh√≠culo/Aeronave</li>
                            <li>Seleccionar Conductor/Piloto</li>
                            <li>Registrar Carga</li>
                            <li>Calcular Costo</li>
                        </ul>
                        <div style="margin-top: 1rem;">
                            <button onclick="closeModal()" style="background: var(--primary); color: white; border: none; padding: 0.5rem 1rem; border-radius: 8px; cursor: pointer;">Continuar</button>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `);
            }, 1000);
        }

        function manageSeguros() {
            showNotification('Gestionando seguros...');
            showModal('Gesti√≥n de Seguros', `
                <div style="line-height: 1.6;">
                    <p>M√≥dulo de gesti√≥n de seguros:</p>
                    <ul>
                        <li>Ver p√≥lizas vigentes</li>
                        <li>Alertas de vencimiento</li>
                        <li>Renovaci√≥n de seguros</li>
                        <li>Documentaci√≥n digital</li>
                        <li>Reportes de cobertura</li>
                    </ul>
                </div>
            `);
        }

        function renewInsurance(vehicleId) {
            showNotification(`Renovando seguro para ${vehicleId}...`);
            closeModal();
            setTimeout(() => {
                showNotification(`‚úì Seguro renovado exitosamente para ${vehicleId}`);
            }, 2000);
        }

        function rescheduleMaintenance(aeronaveId) {
            showNotification(`Reprogramando mantenimiento para ${aeronaveId}...`);
            closeModal();
            setTimeout(() => {
                showNotification(`‚úì Mantenimiento reprogramado para ${aeronaveId}`);
            }, 2000);
        }

        // List View Functions
        function showVehiculosList() {
            goToPage('vehiculos.html');
        }

        function showAeronavesList() {
            goToPage('aeronaves.html');
        }

        function showPersonalList() {
            goToPage('conductores.html');
        }

        function showInsuranceManagement() {
            goToPage('seguros.html');
        }

        // Quick Actions Functions
        function manageVehiculos() {
            goToPage('vehiculos.html');
        }

        function manageClientes() {
            goToPage('clientes.html');
        }

        function manageRutas() {
            goToPage('rutas.html');
        }

        function generateReportes() {
            goToPage('reportes.html');
        }

        // Close modal when clicking outside
        window.onclick = function(event) {
            const modal = document.getElementById('detailsModal');
            if (event.target === modal) {
                closeModal();
            }
        }

        // Simulate real-time updates
        function simulateRealTimeUpdate() {
            const statValues = document.querySelectorAll('.stat-value');
            setInterval(() => {
                const randomStat = statValues[Math.floor(Math.random() * statValues.length)];
                const currentValue = parseInt(randomStat.textContent.replace('$', '').replace('M', '').replace('K', ''));
                const change = Math.random() > 0.5 ? 1 : -1;
                if (!isNaN(currentValue)) {
                    randomStat.style.transform = 'scale(1.1)';
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        randomStat.textContent = currentValue + change;
                        randomStat.style.transform = 'scale(1)';
                    }, 200);
                }
            }, 10000);
        }

        simulateRealTimeUpdate();

        console.log('üöÄ Dashboard Log√≠stica Global cargado exitosamente');
        console.log('üìä Sistema integrado con Django REST Framework');
        console.log('üîê Autenticaci√≥n JWT activa');
        console.log('üõ°Ô∏è M√≥dulo de seguros implementado');
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <script>
        // Modal Functions
        function showModal(modalId) {
            document.getElementById(modalId).style.display = 'block';
        }

        function closeModal(modalId) {
            document.getElementById(modalId).style.display = 'none';
        }

        function showNewDespachoModal() {
            showModal('newDespachoModal');
        }

        // View Despacho Details
        function viewDespacho(despachoId) {
            const content = `
                <div style="line-height: 1.6;">
                    <p><strong>ID:</strong> ${despachoId}</p>
                    <p><strong>Cliente:</strong> TechCorp S.A.</p>
                    <p><strong>Ruta:</strong> Santiago - Valpara√≠so</p>
                    <p><strong>Tipo:</strong> Terrestre</p>
                    <p><strong>Estado:</strong> <span class="badge active">Completado</span></p>
                    <p><strong>Fecha de Creaci√≥n:</strong> 10/12/2023</p>
                    <p><strong>Fecha de Entrega:</strong> 10/12/2023 14:30</p>
                    <p><strong>Veh√≠culo:</strong> CAM-789</p>
                    <p><strong>Conductor:</strong> Carlos L√≥pez</p>
                    <p><strong>Carga:</strong> Electr√≥nicos - 850kg</p>
                    <p><strong>Costo:</strong> $250,000</p>
                    <div style="margin-top: 1.5rem;">
                        <h4>Historial de Estado</h4>
                        <ul style="margin-top: 0.5rem;">
                            <li>10/12/2023 14:30 - Entregado</li>
                            <li>10/12/2023 11:15 - En ruta</li>
                            <li>10/12/2023 08:00 - Cargado</li>
                            <li>09/12/2023 16:00 - Programado</li>
                        </ul>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
            document.getElementById('viewDespachoTitle').textContent = `Despacho ${despachoId}`;
            document.getElementById('viewDespachoContent').innerHTML = content;
            showModal('viewDespachoModal');
        }

        // Edit Despacho
        function editDespacho(despachoId) {
            showNotification(`Editando despacho ${despachoId}...`);
            // In a real application, this would load the edit form with existing data
        }

        // Form Submission
        document.getElementById('newDespachoForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            showNotification('Despacho creado exitosamente');
            closeModal('newDespachoModal');
            // In a real application, this would submit the form data to the server
        });

        // Notification System
        function showNotification(message) {
            const notification = document.createElement('div');
            notification.textContent = `‚úì ${message}`;
            notification.style.cssText = `
                position: fixed;
                top: 20px;
                right: 20px;
                background: linear-gradient(135deg, #6366f1, #06b6d4);
                color: white;
                padding: 1rem 2rem;
                border-radius: 12px;
                box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(99, 102, 241, 0.4);
                z-index: 1000;
                animation: slideInRight 0.4s ease-out;
                font-weight: 600;
            `;
            
            document.body.appendChild(notification);
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                notification.style.animation = 'slideOutRight 0.4s ease-out';
                setTimeout(() => notification.remove(), 400);
            }, 3000);
        }

        // Add slide animations
        const style = document.createElement('style');
        style.textContent = `
            @keyframes slideInRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
            }
            @keyframes slideOutRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
            }
        `;
        document.head.appendChild(style);

        // Close modal when clicking outside
        window.onclick = function(event) {
            const modals = document.querySelectorAll('.modal');
            modals.forEach(modal => {
                if (event.target === modal) {
                    modal.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
        }

        console.log('üì¶ M√≥dulo de Despachos cargado exitosamente');
    </script>

    <script>
        function showModal(modalId) {
            document.getElementById(modalId).style.display = 'block';
        }

        function closeModal(modalId) {
            document.getElementById(modalId).style.display = 'none';
        }

        function showNewPilotoModal() {
            showModal('newPilotoModal');
        }

        function viewPiloto(pilotoId) {
            const content = `
                <div style="line-height: 1.6;">
                    <p><strong>ID:</strong> ${pilotoId}</p>
                    <p><strong>Nombre:</strong> Roberto Silva</p>
                    <p><strong>Licencia:</strong> ATPL</p>
                    <p><strong>Vence Licencia:</strong> 15/06/2024</p>
                    <p><strong>Tel√©fono:</strong> +56 9 1234 5678</p>
                    <p><strong>Email:</strong> roberto.silva@empresa.com</p>
                    <p><strong>Aeronave Asignada:</strong> CC-AW01 (Boeing 737-800F)</p>
                    <p><strong>Estado:</strong> <span class="badge active">Activo</span></p>
                    <p><strong>Horas de Vuelo:</strong> 4,250 hrs</p>
                    <div style="margin-top: 1.5rem;">
                        <h4>Estad√≠sticas</h4>
                        <ul style="margin-top: 0.5rem;">
                            <li>Vuelos este mes: 8</li>
                            <li>Horas voladas: 45 hrs</li>
                            <li>Calificaci√≥n promedio: 4.9/5</li>
                            <li>Incidentes: 0</li>
                        </ul>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
            document.getElementById('viewPilotoTitle').textContent = `Piloto ${pilotoId}`;
            document.getElementById('viewPilotoContent').innerHTML = content;
            showModal('viewPilotoModal');
        }

        function editPiloto(pilotoId) {
            showNotification(`Editando piloto ${pilotoId}...`);
        }

        document.getElementById('newPilotoForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            showNotification('Piloto creado exitosamente');
            closeModal('newPilotoModal');
        });

        function showNotification(message) {
            const notification = document.createElement('div');
            notification.textContent = `‚úì ${message}`;
            notification.style.cssText = `
                position: fixed;
                top: 20px;
                right: 20px;
                background: linear-gradient(135deg, #6366f1, #06b6d4);
                color: white;
                padding: 1rem 2rem;
                border-radius: 12px;
                box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(99, 102, 241, 0.4);
                z-index: 1000;
                animation: slideInRight 0.4s ease-out;
                font-weight: 600;
            `;
            
            document.body.appendChild(notification);
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                notification.style.animation = 'slideOutRight 0.4s ease-out';
                setTimeout(() => notification.remove(), 400);
            }, 3000);
        }

        const style = document.createElement('style');
        style.textContent = `
            @keyframes slideInRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
            }
            @keyframes slideOutRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
            }
        `;
        document.head.appendChild(style);

        window.onclick = function(event) {
            const modals = document.querySelectorAll('.modal');
            modals.forEach(modal => {
                if (event.target === modal) {
                    modal.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
        }

        console.log('üë®‚Äç‚úàÔ∏è M√≥dulo de Pilotos cargado exitosamente');
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <script>
        function generateReport(tipo) {
            showNotification(`Generando reporte de ${tipo}...`);
            // Simulate report generation
            setTimeout(() => {
                showNotification(`‚úì Reporte de ${tipo} generado exitosamente`);
            }, 2000);
        }

        function viewReport(reportId) {
            showNotification(`Visualizando reporte ${reportId}...`);
            // In a real application, this would open the report in a modal or new tab
        }

        function downloadReport(reportId) {
            showNotification(`Descargando reporte ${reportId}...`);
            // In a real application, this would trigger the download
        }

        function regenerateReport(reportId) {
            showNotification(`Regenerando reporte ${reportId}...`);
            // In a real application, this would regenerate the report
            setTimeout(() => {
                showNotification(`‚úì Reporte ${reportId} regenerado exitosamente`);
            }, 2000);
        }

        function showNewReportModal() {
            showNotification('Abriendo generador de reportes personalizados...');
            // In a real application, this would open a modal for custom report generation
        }

        function showNotification(message) {
            const notification = document.createElement('div');
            notification.textContent = `‚úì ${message}`;
            notification.style.cssText = `
                position: fixed;
                top: 20px;
                right: 20px;
                background: linear-gradient(135deg, #6366f1, #06b6d4);
                color: white;
                padding: 1rem 2rem;
                border-radius: 12px;
                box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(99, 102, 241, 0.4);
                z-index: 1000;
                animation: slideInRight 0.4s ease-out;
                font-weight: 600;
            `;
            
            document.body.appendChild(notification);
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                notification.style.animation = 'slideOutRight 0.4s ease-out';
                setTimeout(() => notification.remove(), 400);
            }, 3000);
        }

        const style = document.createElement('style');
        style.textContent = `
            @keyframes slideInRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
            }
            @keyframes slideOutRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
            }
        `;
        document.head.appendChild(style);

        console.log('üìà M√≥dulo de Reportes cargado exitosamente');
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <script>
        function showModal(modalId) {
            document.getElementById(modalId).style.display = 'block';
        }

        function closeModal(modalId) {
            document.getElementById(modalId).style.display = 'none';
        }

        function showNewRutaModal() {
            showModal('newRutaModal');
        }

        function viewRuta(rutaId) {
            const content = `
                <div style="line-height: 1.6;">
                    <p><strong>ID:</strong> ${rutaId}</p>
                    <p><strong>Origen:</strong> Santiago</p>
                    <p><strong>Destino:</strong> Valpara√≠so</p>
                    <p><strong>Tipo:</strong> Terrestre</p>
                    <p><strong>Distancia:</strong> 120 km</p>
                    <p><strong>Tiempo Estimado:</strong> 2h 15m</p>
                    <p><strong>Estado:</strong> <span class="badge active">Activa</span></p>
                    <p><strong>Descripci√≥n:</strong> Ruta principal entre Santiago y Valpara√≠so</p>
                    <div style="margin-top: 1.5rem;">
                        <h4>Estad√≠sticas</h4>
                        <ul style="margin-top: 0.5rem;">
                            <li>Despachos este mes: 42</li>
                            <li>Tiempo promedio real: 2h 20m</li>
                            <li>Porcentaje de √©xito: 98%</li>
                        </ul>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
            document.getElementById('viewRutaTitle').textContent = `Ruta ${rutaId}`;
            document.getElementById('viewRutaContent').innerHTML = content;
            showModal('viewRutaModal');
        }

        function editRuta(rutaId) {
            showNotification(`Editando ruta ${rutaId}...`);
        }

        document.getElementById('newRutaForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            showNotification('Ruta creada exitosamente');
            closeModal('newRutaModal');
        });

        function showNotification(message) {
            const notification = document.createElement('div');
            notification.textContent = `‚úì ${message}`;
            notification.style.cssText = `
                position: fixed;
                top: 20px;
                right: 20px;
                background: linear-gradient(135deg, #6366f1, #06b6d4);
                color: white;
                padding: 1rem 2rem;
                border-radius: 12px;
                box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(99, 102, 241, 0.4);
                z-index: 1000;
                animation: slideInRight 0.4s ease-out;
                font-weight: 600;
            `;
            
            document.body.appendChild(notification);
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                notification.style.animation = 'slideOutRight 0.4s ease-out';
                setTimeout(() => notification.remove(), 400);
            }, 3000);
        }

        const style = document.createElement('style');
        style.textContent = `
            @keyframes slideInRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
            }
            @keyframes slideOutRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
            }
        `;
        document.head.appendChild(style);

        window.onclick = function(event) {
            const modals = document.querySelectorAll('.modal');
            modals.forEach(modal => {
                if (event.target === modal) {
                    modal.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
        }

        console.log('üó∫Ô∏è M√≥dulo de Rutas cargado exitosamente');
    </script>
</body>
</html>
============================================================

                    <button type="submit" class="btn">Crear Seguro</button>
                </div>
            </form>
        </div>
    </div>

    <div id="viewSeguroModal" class="modal">
        <div class="modal-content">
            <span class="close-modal" onclick="closeModal('viewSeguroModal')">&times;</span>
            <h3 id="viewSeguroTitle">Detalles del Seguro</h3>
            <div id="viewSeguroContent"></div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        function showModal(modalId) {
            document.getElementById(modalId).style.display = 'block';
        }

        function closeModal(modalId) {
            document.getElementById(modalId).style.display = 'none';
        }

        function showNewSeguroModal() {
            showModal('newSeguroModal');
        }

        function viewSeguro(poliza) {
            const content = `
                <div style="line-height: 1.6;">
                    <p><strong>P√≥liza:</strong> ${poliza}</p>
                    <p><strong>Asegurado:</strong> ABC-123 (Veh√≠culo - Volvo FH16)</p>
                    <p><strong>Tipo:</strong> Veh√≠culo</p>
                    <p><strong>Aseguradora:</strong> Seguros Chile</p>
                    <p><strong>Cobertura:</strong> $500,000</p>
                    <p><strong>Prima Anual:</strong> $5,000</p>
                    <p><strong>Vigencia Desde:</strong> 15/01/2023</p>
                    <p><strong>Vigencia Hasta:</strong> 15/01/2024</p>
                    <p><strong>D√≠as Restantes:</strong> 32 d√≠as</p>
                    <p><strong>Estado:</strong> <span class="badge active">Vigente</span></p>
                    <p><strong>Observaciones:</strong> Cobertura completa incluye responsabilidad civil</p>
                    <div style="margin-top: 1.5rem;">
                        <h4>Coberturas Incluidas</h4>
                        <ul style="margin-top: 0.5rem;">
                            <li>Da√±os totales y parciales</li>
                            <li>Responsabilidad civil</li>
                            <li>Robo total</li>
                            <li>Incendio</li>
                            <li>Asistencia en carretera</li>
                        </ul>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
            document.getElementById('viewSeguroTitle').textContent = `Seguro ${poliza}`;
            document.getElementById('viewSeguroContent').innerHTML = content;
            showModal('viewSeguroModal');
        }

        function editSeguro(poliza) {
            showNotification(`Editando seguro ${poliza}...`);
        }

        document.getElementById('newSeguroForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            showNotification('Seguro creado exitosamente');
            closeModal('newSeguroModal');
        });

        function showNotification(message) {
            const notification = document.createElement('div');
            notification.textContent = `‚úì ${message}`;
            notification.style.cssText = `
                position: fixed;
                top: 20px;
                right: 20px;
                background: linear-gradient(135deg, #6366f1, #06b6d4);
                color: white;
                padding: 1rem 2rem;
                border-radius: 12px;
                box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(99, 102, 241, 0.4);
                z-index: 1000;
                animation: slideInRight 0.4s ease-out;
                font-weight: 600;
            `;
            
            document.body.appendChild(notification);
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                notification.style.animation = 'slideOutRight 0.4s ease-out';
                setTimeout(() => notification.remove(), 400);
            }, 3000);
        }

        const style = document.createElement('style');
        style.textContent = `
            @keyframes slideInRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
            }
            @keyframes slideOutRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
            }
        `;
        document.head.appendChild(style);

        window.onclick = function(event) {
            const modals = document.querySelectorAll('.modal');
            modals.forEach(modal => {
                if (event.target === modal) {
                    modal.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
        }

        console.log('üõ°Ô∏è M√≥dulo de Seguros cargado exitosamente');
    </script>
</body>
</html>

        <div class="modal-content">
            <span class="close-modal" onclick="closeModal('viewVehiculoModal')">&times;</span>
            <h3 id="viewVehiculoTitle">Detalles del Veh√≠culo</h3>
            <div id="viewVehiculoContent"></div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        function showModal(modalId) {
            document.getElementById(modalId).style.display = 'block';
        }

        function closeModal(modalId) {
            document.getElementById(modalId).style.display = 'none';
        }

        function showNewVehiculoModal() {
            showModal('newVehiculoModal');
        }

        function viewVehiculo(patente) {
            const content = `
                <div style="line-height: 1.6;">
                    <p><strong>Patente:</strong> ${patente}</p>
                    <p><strong>Modelo:</strong> Volvo FH16</p>
                    <p><strong>Tipo:</strong> Cami√≥n</p>
                    <p><strong>Capacidad:</strong> 25 toneladas</p>
                    <p><strong>A√±o:</strong> 2022</p>
                    <p><strong>Conductor:</strong> Carlos L√≥pez</p>
                    <p><strong>Estado:</strong> <span class="badge active">Activo</span></p>
                    <p><strong>√öltimo Mantenimiento:</strong> 01/12/2023</p>
                    <p><strong>Pr√≥ximo Mantenimiento:</strong> 01/01/2024</p>
                    <div style="margin-top: 1.5rem;">
                        <h4>Seguro</h4>
                        <ul style="margin-top: 0.5rem;">
                            <li>Aseguradora: Seguros Chile</li>
                            <li>P√≥liza: #SC-2023-${patente}</li>
                            <li>Vencimiento: 15/01/2024</li>
                            <li>Estado: <span class="badge active">Vigente</span></li>
                        </ul>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
            document.getElementById('viewVehiculoTitle').textContent = `Veh√≠culo ${patente}`;
            document.getElementById('viewVehiculoContent').innerHTML = content;
            showModal('viewVehiculoModal');
        }

        function editVehiculo(patente) {
            showNotification(`Editando veh√≠culo ${patente}...`);
        }

        document.getElementById('newVehiculoForm').addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            showNotification('Veh√≠culo creado exitosamente');
            closeModal('newVehiculoModal');
        });

        function showNotification(message) {
            const notification = document.createElement('div');
            notification.textContent = `‚úì ${message}`;
            notification.style.cssText = `
                position: fixed;
                top: 20px;
                right: 20px;
                background: linear-gradient(135deg, #6366f1, #06b6d4);
                color: white;
                padding: 1rem 2rem;
                border-radius: 12px;
                box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(99, 102, 241, 0.4);
                z-index: 1000;
                animation: slideInRight 0.4s ease-out;
                font-weight: 600;
            `;
            
            document.body.appendChild(notification);
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                notification.style.animation = 'slideOutRight 0.4s ease-out';
                setTimeout(() => notification.remove(), 400);
            }, 3000);
        }

        const style = document.createElement('style');
        style.textContent = `
            @keyframes slideInRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
            }
            @keyframes slideOutRight {
                from {
                    transform: translateX(0);
                    opacity: 1;
                }
                to {
                    transform: translateX(400px);
                    opacity: 0;
                }
            }
        `;
        document.head.appendChild(style);

        window.onclick = function(event) {
            const modals = document.querySelectorAll('.modal');
            modals.forEach(modal => {
                if (event.target === modal) {
                    modal.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
        }

        console.log('üöõ M√≥dulo de Veh√≠culos cargado exitosamente');
    </script>
</body>
